CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Leaves_CarryForward](
	[Id] [int] IDENTITY(1,1) PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL,
	[EmpId] [int] NULL,
	[LeaveTypeId] [int] NULL,
	[Year] [int] NULL,
	[CarryForward] [int] NULL,
	[LeaveCredit] [int] NULL,
	[LeaveDebit] [int] NULL,
	[LeaveBalance] [int] NULL);
	
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Leaves_CarryForward]  WITH CHECK ADD  CONSTRAINT [FK_Leaves_CarryForward_Employees] FOREIGN KEY([EmpId])
REFERENCES [dbo].[Employees] ([Id]);

ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Leaves_CarryForward]  WITH CHECK ADD  CONSTRAINT [FK_Leaves_CarryForward_Leavetypes] FOREIGN KEY([LeaveTypeId])
REFERENCES [dbo].[LeaveTypes] ([Id]);

CREATE  View [dbo].[V_LeaveForward]
as
(select CAST(ROW_NUMBER() over(order by l.Id desc) AS INT) Id,
(select distinct l.EmpId) as EmpId,CONCAT(e.FirstName,' ',e.Lastname) as EmpName,d.Name as DeptName,dg.Name as DesignationName,b.name as BranchName,l.Leavecredit,
l.Leavedebit,l.Year,l.LeaveBalance,l.CarryForward,l.leavetypeid,
(select isnull(sum(l1.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l1 where l1.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Casual Leave')) as CasualLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l2.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l2 where l2.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Medical/Sick Leave')) as MedicalSickLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l3.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l3 where l3.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Privilege Leave')) as PrivilegeLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l4.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l4 where l4.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Maternity Leave')) as MaternityLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l5.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l5 where l5.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Paternity Leave')) as PaternityLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l6.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l6 where l6.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Extraordinary Leave')) as ExtraordinaryLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l7.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l7 where l7.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Special Casual Leave')) as SpecialCasualLeave,
(select isnull(sum(l8.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l8 where l8.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Compensatory Off')) as CompensatoryOff,
(select isnull(sum(l9.LeaveBalance),0) from Leaves_CarryForward l9 where l9.EmpId=l.empid  and LeaveTypeId = (select Id from [LeaveTypes] where Type='Loss of Pay')) as LOP
from Leaves_CarryForward l join employees e on e.id=l.empid join Departments d on e.department=d.id join designations dg on e.currentdesignation=dg.id
join branches b on e.branch=b.id) 



CREATE view [dbo].[V_EmpLeavesCarryForward] as
WITH cte AS
(
   SELECT *,ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY empID ORDER BY empid DESC) as RowId FROM V_LeaveForward
)
SELECT * FROM cte WHERE RowId = 1
